\hypertarget{ni__device__api_8h}{}\section{ni\+\_\+device\+\_\+api.\+h File Reference}
\label{ni__device__api_8h}\index{ni\_device\_api.h@{ni\_device\_api.h}}


Main N\+E\+T\+I\+NT device A\+PI header file provides the ability to communicate with NI T-\/408 type hardware transcoder devices.

\subsection{Detailed Description}
Main N\+E\+T\+I\+NT device A\+PI header file provides the ability to communicate with NI T-\/408 type hardware transcoder devices. 





\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
(c) 2019 N\+E\+T\+I\+NT Technologies Inc. All rights reserved. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
